width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;501&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"501\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-e767014d898310d04085ef875fefb600_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-e767014d898310d04085ef875fefb600_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>上面讲的这个人您可能不熟悉，其实历史上的很多名人都有洁癖，例如<b>宋代的大书法家米芾就有，</b>每天吃饭前必须洗手七八次，而且无论走到哪里都会带一个仆人，拎着水壶以方便自己随时洗手。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-92907113464d7032f7e2fc2e753fb16d_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"285\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-92907113464d7032f7e2fc2e753fb16d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;285&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"285\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-92907113464d7032f7e2fc2e753fb16d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-92907113464d7032f7e2fc2e753fb16d_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>有一次他得到了一个绝世的砚台，好友周仁熟知道后也想据为己有，就让米芾把宝贝拿出来秀一下，周仁熟见到后吐口唾沫就开始研墨，<b>米芾看到之后洁癖症大爆发，</b>瞬间觉得这方砚已经被玷污了，于是周仁熟成功的把这方砚拿走了。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-e39683338062d4e13c4d0f25a39c3502_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"340\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-e39683338062d4e13c4d0f25a39c3502_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;340&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"340\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-e39683338062d4e13c4d0f25a39c3502_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-e39683338062d4e13c4d0f25a39c3502_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>米芾还把“洁癖”移植到嫁女儿上，当时有一个读书人叫段拂，字去尘，米芾听说之后非常的开心，觉得这个名字非常的干净，<b>直接就把自己的女儿嫁给了他，</b>尼玛，这种神操作居然也有！</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-78ad14bf83597833629ba32d1281f58d_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"900\" data-rawheight=\"232\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"900\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-78ad14bf83597833629ba32d1281f58d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;687&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"687\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-05e05d74a606dc653df7c1513a4508ed_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-05e05d74a606dc653df7c1513a4508ed_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>当然还有比米芾更加夸张的，<b>元朝末年大画家倪瓒是个“洁癖狂”。</b>光每天洗头洗澡就得十几次，而且他连厕所都得上香厕，用香木搭好格子，中间铺上洁白的鹅毛，然后才能安心的拉粑粑。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-58892c11cb9cd3dab4a71d5b83180312_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"900\" data-rawheight=\"156\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"900\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-58892c11cb9cd3dab4a71d5b83180312_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;900&#39; height=&#39;156&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"900\" data-rawheight=\"156\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"900\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-58892c11cb9cd3dab4a71d5b83180312_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-58892c11cb9cd3dab4a71d5b83180312_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f0d2ab8384251b330e0fcf2990b8b6c0_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"666\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f0d2ab8384251b330e0fcf2990b8b6c0_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;666&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"666\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f0d2ab8384251b330e0fcf2990b8b6c0_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f0d2ab8384251b330e0fcf2990b8b6c0_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>他非常喜欢院里的一颗梧桐树，但是觉得这棵梧桐树太脏了，于是每天愣<b>给这颗树洗N遍桑拿，</b>最后洗着洗着就把树给洗死了！</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3d5e712d4d17ffadbbe990e16051ed9d_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"599\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3d5e712d4d17ffadbbe990e16051ed9d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;599&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"599\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3d5e712d4d17ffadbbe990e16051ed9d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3d5e712d4d17ffadbbe990e16051ed9d_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>更奇葩的是他对喝茶也很讲究，仆人从山里挑来的山泉水，他一直只用前面那桶水煎茶，有人问他原因，他给出了理由：后面那桶水可能被仆人放屁污染了，所以不能喝，只配用来洗脚！</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-9b3ca6ed114870822bf355e0097720b2_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"518\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-9b3ca6ed114870822bf355e0097720b2_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;518&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"518\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-9b3ca6ed114870822bf355e0097720b2_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-9b3ca6ed114870822bf355e0097720b2_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>因为洁癖倪瓒成了一枚单身汪，有一天寂寞难耐的他看上个歌妓，于是就带着这个歌姬回家过夜，<b>但又担心歌妓身上不干净，</b>就让歌妓洗澡，洗完后还是不放心，仔细检查后，再让歌妓去洗澡，结果反复洗到了天亮~</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-17d6bec68877716cc6bd7680397a37d6_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"292\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-17d6bec68877716cc6bd7680397a37d6_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;292&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"292\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-17d6bec68877716cc6bd7680397a37d6_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-17d6bec68877716cc6bd7680397a37d6_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ce252449a934813717c05d667776b208_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"407\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ce252449a934813717c05d667776b208_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;492&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"492\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-7627866d5dcf6c9f34d02b9f8210422c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-7627866d5dcf6c9f34d02b9f8210422c_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>上面这些“洁癖狂”已经够奇葩了，古代还有因为有洁癖而死的人，例如<b>清朝有一个人叫马葵，</b>隔一会儿就得换一次衣服，生怕自己的汗沾到衣服上弄脏，最后觉得洁癖太严重活不下去，就打算找条河投河自杀，却又嫌河水脏，只能找棵树吊死！</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-773f34c6164784013b9e08c30118b140_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"558\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-773f34c6164784013b9e08c30118b140_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;558&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"558\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-773f34c6164784013b9e08c30118b140_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-773f34c6164784013b9e08c30118b140_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>再来看看<b>因洁癖而死的君王—邾庄公，</b>有一天邾庄公站在门台上远眺，突然看到庭院中有一滩形状可疑的水，一查才知道是夷射姑在这里小便，邾庄公大怒，命人抓捕夷射姑，不过夷射姑听到消息事先逃跑了，邾庄公听闻之后气得暴跳如雷，结果一不小心从床上掉进了炭炉里，被烧得体无完肤，最后伤重去世~</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-c700ea86ac5f8960a82707a6066e76e6_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"225\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-c700ea86ac5f8960a82707a6066e76e6_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;225&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"225\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-c700ea86ac5f8960a82707a6066e76e6_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-c700ea86ac5f8960a82707a6066e76e6_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7e917989cf7e2a98388c5d07a16884b6_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"560\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7e917989cf7e2a98388c5d07a16884b6_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;             "content": "<p></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-18948817011a8d448abb80c32fc110cd_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"162\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-18948817011a8d448abb80c32fc110cd_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;588&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"588\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-fbf2093015d93eb6450a1c36131a9ba6_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-fbf2093015d93eb6450a1c36131a9ba6_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>人人都知道魏延脑后有反骨，知道他在长沙归降刘备，诸葛亮疑心不肯收，要将他斩首防患于未然，结果被刘备保了下来！</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-7d4152c98939d4b687a1d7a33576b629_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"590\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-7d4152c98939d4b687a1d7a33576b629_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;590&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"590\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-7d4152c98939d4b687a1d7a33576b629_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-7d4152c98939d4b687a1d7a33576b629_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>还知道诸葛亮尸骨未寒，魏延就发动叛乱，结果被马岱依计诛杀，大家纷纷感慨。丞相果然英明神武，明察秋毫，但实际上，完全不是这么回事！</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-f7fb09c6e880a29769a8728fe1af83a9_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-f7fb09c6e880a29769a8728fe1af83a9_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;640&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-f7fb09c6e880a29769a8728fe1af83a9_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-f7fb09c6e880a29769a8728fe1af83a9_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>首先，魏延根本不是降将，而是一直跟着刘备的亲信，所以刘备对魏延非常信任，也非常的看重。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-da8b4b036573ba11f26831d2acddf5d5_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"103\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-da8b4b036573ba11f26831d2acddf5d5_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;103&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"103\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-da8b4b036573ba11f26831d2acddf5d5_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-da8b4b036573ba11f26831d2acddf5d5_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>刘备在汉中称王的时候，魏延任督汉中镇远将军、领汉中太守，这个位置有多重要呢？当时普遍认为“无汉中则无蜀”。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5bcb3a82128a370b489fbea9f0b1e8b7_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"619\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5bcb3a82128a370b489fbea9f0b1e8b7_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;619&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"619\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5bcb3a82128a370b489fbea9f0b1e8b7_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5bcb3a82128a370b489fbea9f0b1e8b7_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>按理说以桃园结义的关系，这个位置非张飞莫属，谁也没想到会落到魏延身上，可见刘备对魏延的器重！</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-86990271ee038c900ec0fdc5d3e86c18_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"506\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-86990271ee038c900ec0fdc5d3e86c18_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;506&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"506\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-86990271ee038c900ec0fdc5d3e86c18_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-86990271ee038c900ec0fdc5d3e86c18_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>刘备死后，诸葛亮成为蜀地一把手，从公元227年到234年之间，他一共组织了六次北伐，魏延全部参与，其中第四次是由他担纲主帅并大获全胜！</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-53b1e5d40c5dfc3944c4e17c9743c7fa_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"574\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-53b1e5d40c5dfc3944c4e17c9743c7fa_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;574&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"574\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-53b1e5d40c5dfc3944c4e17c9743c7fa_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-53b1e5d40c5dfc3944c4e17c9743c7fa_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>魏延的确不负刘备厚望，反而诸葛亮连连失利，甚至因战败自贬为右将军，也正是在北伐中两人的矛盾集中爆发了，主要的原因就是性格的不同和战略的不同！</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-526525896ae7f0e29f2e2aad49f17b8b_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"588\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-526525896ae7f0e29f2e2aad49f17b8b_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;588&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"588\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-526525896ae7f0e29f2e2aad49f17b8b_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-526525896ae7f0e29f2e2aad49f17b8b_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>我们都知道“诸葛一生唯谨慎”，诸葛亮用兵一贯是稳打稳扎，而魏延则喜欢“出奇制胜”，所以诸葛亮常常压制魏延的计谋！</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-b72026e9f8648564deeee99e835887f7_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"163\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-b72026e9f8648564deeee99e835887f7_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;163&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"163\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-b72026e9f8648564deeee99e835887f7_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-b72026e9f8648564deeee99e835887f7_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>意见不同本来是挺正常的事，但是不要忘了魏延是谁。是战功赫赫又曾深受刘备信任的大将，甚至在当时蜀军大营里流传着。诸葛亮死后应该由魏延继续领导北伐，而魏延也一直以此自许！</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3e84bae449ec0848ddcd85bf15672fda_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"106\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3e84bae449ec0848ddcd85bf15672fda_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;106&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"106\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3e84bae449ec0848ddcd85bf15672fda_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3e84bae449ec0848ddcd85bf15672fda_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-aeae8d191ecfb1c828060f8e59deb7ca_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"565\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-aeae8d191ecfb1c828060f8e59deb7ca_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;565&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"565\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-aeae8d191ecfb1c828060f8e59deb7ca_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-aeae8d191ecfb1c828060f8e59deb7ca_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>而诸葛亮最担心的就是，有人不遵循他的既定方针，所以魏延成了他的一个心腹大患！看看诸葛亮身后事的安排就明白了，撤退时命令魏延断后。如果魏延不服从命令，军队就不管魏延，自行出发，而主持执行诸葛亮命令的人，偏偏又是和他“有如水火”的杨仪！</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-127f536d3f9c7b46ef24e22bda0b86ff_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"686\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-127f536d3f9c7b46ef24e22bda0b86ff_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;686&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"686\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-127f536d3f9c7b46ef24e22bda0b86ff_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-127f536d3f9c7b46ef24e22bda0b86ff_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>所以魏延得到消息之后非常生气，感觉自己被完全排挤到了核心圈外：</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4c4dfe0fb266425965c6138313011472_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"226\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4c4dfe0fb266425965c6138313011472_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;226&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"226\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4c4dfe0fb266425965c6138313011472_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4c4dfe0fb266425965c6138313011472_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>替别人断后扫尾，除了面子上过不去之外，还陷入了一种两难的境地，如果完全遵循诸葛亮的政治安排，回到蜀国后，杨仪掌权肯定会秋后算账，如果不遵循诸葛亮的政治遗嘱。杨仪就会带着主力军撤回，魏延就要以偏军面对司马懿大军！</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-2f3f3d1efc52d1f29ccce2937a2a40b2_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"572\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-2f3f3d1efc52d1f29ccce2937a2a40b2_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;572&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"572\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-2f3f3d1efc52d1f29ccce2937a2a40b2_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-2f3f3d1efc52d1f29ccce2937a2a40b2_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>这个时候魏延就走了一步臭棋，他自己率领所部先行撤退了，而且还把栈道全部烧毁，以阻止杨仪的部队撤退，同时还上表奏告杨仪谋逆~</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6853ab03ae5ab7b669a874c4ddb17a9d_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"462\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6853ab03ae5ab7b669a874c4ddb17a9d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;462&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"462\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6853ab03ae5ab7b669a874c4ddb17a9d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6853ab03ae5ab7b669a874c4ddb17a9d_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>此时杨仪也揭发魏延要造反，而杨仪在道义上更站得住脚，因为他执行的是诸葛亮的命令，而魏延的做法正好给了他理由！</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-30df565f61997ff2a109a03532c2b7c1_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"506\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-30df565f61997ff2a109a03532c2b7c1_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;506&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"506\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-30df565f61997ff2a109a03532c2b7c1_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-30df565f61997ff2a109a03532c2b7c1_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>所以杨仪派兵抵抗魏延的阻击，并且向魏延部下伸张国家大义，魏延的部下随即一哄而散，而魏延最终也被马岱的追兵斩杀，一代名将就这样被自己人干掉了！这就是所谓的“反骨”的故事。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f75c3c80da637a5d9f232d7db486de87_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"614\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f75c3c80da637a5d9f232d7db486de87_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;614&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"614\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f75c3c80da637a5d9f232d7db486de87_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f75c3c80da637a5d9f232d7db486de87_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>魏延的死其实是一个冤假错案，无论是历史学家陈寿的《三国志》，还是裴松之的《三国志注》，都认为魏延没有谋反之心！</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-45e0bd3def7724ba996c571c1d5852b7_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"603\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-45e0bd3def7724ba996c571c1d5852b7_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;603&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"603\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-45e0bd3def7724ba996c571c1d5852b7_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-45e0bd3def7724ba996c571c1d5852b7_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>不得不说魏延的死，诸葛亮负有很大的责任。他在掌握蜀汉实权之后，可以说是“事事亲力亲为”，如果有人的政治意见和他不同，就会遭到全面的“封杀”，这就严重阻碍了后进人才的发挥！</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-8eeca3c7a55a69a009dac06dea2a250c_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"495\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-8eeca3c7a55a69a009dac06dea2a250c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;183&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"183\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-773132d1e7a16ec1f9cb7d8e25b1aa48_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-773132d1e7a16ec1f9cb7d8e25b1aa48_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>诸葛亮胸怀天下，器宇不凡，王朗也是心胸宽阔，有容乃大，虽然地盘被孙策给占了，但王司徒一点都不感到委屈，甚至还给仇家点了个赞，告诉曹操，孙策是一个好领导，江东地区千万<b>不能小看。</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-2cf04bcba8c1c01d66d8c6372d657e5e_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"284\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-2cf04bcba8c1c01d66d8c6372d657e5e_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;284&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"284\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-2cf04bcba8c1c01d66d8c6372d657e5e_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-2cf04bcba8c1c01d66d8c6372d657e5e_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-715765966a562fb1604f813c5ef184d1_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"183\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-715765966a562fb1604f813c5ef184d1_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;183&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"183\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-715765966a562fb1604f813c5ef184d1_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-715765966a562fb1604f813c5ef184d1_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>诸葛亮是著名的政治家，而王朗在政治上也做过贡献，有一段时间曹操想恢复古代的肉刑，即割鼻子、挖膝盖等残酷的刑法，大臣钟繇非常赞成这提案，但是王司徒却<b>坚决反对，</b>认为这种刑罚太过于残忍。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-65e5948c55d8ba6f97f62d5d16d2f9b2_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"450\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-65e5948c55d8ba6f97f62d5d16d2f9b2_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;450&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"450\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-65e5948c55d8ba6f97f62d5d16d2f9b2_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-65e5948c55d8ba6f97f62d5d16d2f9b2_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-1acf56f1116e3e85a4abbe5288e5d9ae_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"183\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-1acf56f1116e3e85a4abbe5288e5d9ae_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;183&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"183\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-1acf56f1116e3e85a4abbe5288e5d9ae_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-1acf56f1116e3e85a4abbe5288e5d9ae_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>诸葛亮可以称得上是一个文学家，《出师表》、《诫子书》都是经典，而王朗更是博学多闻，是当时的<b>学术大咖。</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-aa7bf1e9aaf33e2b5024e13de6630156_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"497\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-aa7bf1e9aaf33e2b5024e13de6630156_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;497&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"497\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-aa7bf1e9aaf33e2b5024e13de6630156_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-aa7bf1e9aaf33e2b5024e13de6630156_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>在中国古代学术圈想要站稳脚跟，首先就要在经学上抢到注释权，在这一点王朗做到了极致，他通过校注儒家经典，获得了极高的人气，正始六年，王朗的《周易传》，成为了学习周易的人的<b>必读参考书。</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6fdac322d7add94cec13a680c490f999_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"169\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6fdac322d7add94cec13a680c490f999_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;169&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"169\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6fdac322d7add94cec13a680c490f999_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6fdac322d7add94cec13a680c490f999_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-c449896a7cef86a1b18f5ecb9cf1264e_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"183\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-c449896a7cef86a1b18f5ecb9cf1264e_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;183&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"183\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-c449896a7cef86a1b18f5ecb9cf1264e_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-c449896a7cef86a1b18f5ecb9cf1264e_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>最后再来比拼一下后代，诸葛亮虽然很牛逼，但他的几个儿子却不怎么争气，在这一点上王司徒就比较成功了，他最大的骄傲就是儿子<b>王肃，</b>王肃完全继承了老爹的衣钵，写了一大堆书，《尚书传》、《孔子家语》、《孔丛子》，成为了一个著名的经学家 。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-42b6050e00edf3fb07ce825b80acebeb_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"600\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-42b6050e00edf3fb07ce825b80acebeb_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;600&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"600\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-42b6050e00edf3fb07ce825b80acebeb_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-42b6050e00edf3fb07ce825b80acebeb_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>而他的孙女王元姬更厉害，最后嫁给了晋王司马昭，生下了晋武帝司马炎，所以论辈分王朗还是晋武帝的<b>太爷爷。</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-490ffad8343902e5547fa2dc14c6e8ba_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"573\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-490ffad8343902e5547fa2dc14c6e8ba_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;573&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"573\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-490ffad8343902e5547fa2dc14c6e8ba_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-490ffad8343902e5547fa2dc14c6e8ba_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>而且他这个孙女<b>很有眼光，</b>她很早就预言钟会将会造反，劝诫司马昭不要重用钟会，一定要防备防备再防备，后来钟会灭了蜀汉之后，果然拉起大旗造反了！</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6eed6253633faa3195b82a1daccfaa2a_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"629\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6eed6253633faa3195b82a1daccfaa2a_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;413&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"413\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f6f176edf442bc143e3c349e8f8386cc_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f6f176edf442bc143e3c349e8f8386cc_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>如果王朗在九泉之下见到诸葛亮，是不是也可以向他吹牛逼：你不是一直想灭魏国吗？我曾孙子司马炎把曹魏给灭了！钟会不是把你们蜀汉给灭了吗？我孙女儿给你们蜀汉<b>报仇</b>啦！是不是该感谢我一下！</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-c5eccd85de07700dc93942846a0908d2_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"694\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-c5eccd85de07700dc93942846a0908d2_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;162&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"162\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5487b7221fab240567c74b17bca6b193_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5487b7221fab240567c74b17bca6b193_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>《金瓶梅》大家应该并不陌生，甚至对于<b>某些情节</b>特别熟悉。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7ffa31fa9da4e7d6922e6b0552d559cf_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"505\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7ffa31fa9da4e7d6922e6b0552d559cf_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;505&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"505\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7ffa31fa9da4e7d6922e6b0552d559cf_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7ffa31fa9da4e7d6922e6b0552d559cf_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>不过大部分人都是通过<b>电影。</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a603ab2d4f31361fbaff382148c7b311_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"426\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a603ab2d4f31361fbaff382148c7b311_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;426&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"426\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a603ab2d4f31361fbaff382148c7b311_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a603ab2d4f31361fbaff382148c7b311_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a4f6a6e52c1d91b3be685ea4ce00ad79_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"442\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a4f6a6e52c1d91b3be685ea4ce00ad79_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;442&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"442\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a4f6a6e52c1d91b3be685ea4ce00ad79_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a4f6a6e52c1d91b3be685ea4ce00ad79_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>或者对于小说里的<b>插图</b>来了解的。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-48c90048e9f20f9d5b59fea1047811d2_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"427\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-48c90048e9f20f9d5b59fea1047811d2_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;427&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"427\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-48c90048e9f20f9d5b59fea1047811d2_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-48c90048e9f20f9d5b59fea1047811d2_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>而对小说本身并没有太大的兴趣，其实小说远比电影要好看，而且更加具有<b>人生的哲理，</b>也更加的耐人寻味。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b609aa932aa6e5caaeb9a0c3c0ebd14a_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"727\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b609aa932aa6e5caaeb9a0c3c0ebd14a_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;727&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"727\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b609aa932aa6e5caaeb9a0c3c0ebd14a_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b609aa932aa6e5caaeb9a0c3c0ebd14a_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>《金瓶梅》是三个人名字的缩写，即潘金莲、李瓶儿、庞春梅，这三个人也是这本书里的三个女猪脚，《金瓶梅》讲述的故事也很简单，描写的是清河县无赖<b>西门庆，</b>如何发家致富，放纵欲望，最终身死命殒，家道衰败的故事，当然《金瓶梅》最精彩的，就是西门庆集齐<b>七颗龙珠</b>的故事了。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-e1fc433d78b41ade22cec447dc87bbe7_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"568\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-e1fc433d78b41ade22cec447dc87bbe7_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;568&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"568\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-e1fc433d78b41ade22cec447dc87bbe7_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-e1fc433d78b41ade22cec447dc87bbe7_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>第一颗龙珠就是<b>吴月娘，</b>吴月娘是西门庆的原配，是清河县武装部部长吴千户的女儿，为人温柔善良、脾气和顺，对西门庆也非常体贴和关心。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b8b2f945b86b2f3bbc4c461d660a53ee_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"524\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b8b2f945b86b2f3bbc4c461d660a53ee_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;524&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"524\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b8b2f945b86b2f3bbc4c461d660a53ee_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b8b2f945b86b2f3bbc4c461d660a53ee_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>第二颗龙珠就是<b>李娇儿，</b>这个人是酒吧的失足少女，后来被西门庆带回家做了妾。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-f7ace37cd21f2f3c663fbb60ed6a12ba_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"503\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-f7ace37cd21f2f3c663fbb60ed6a12ba_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;503&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"503\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-f7ace37cd21f2f3c663fbb60ed6a12ba_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-f7ace37cd21f2f3c663fbb60ed6a12ba_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>第三颗龙珠是<b>孟玉楼，</b>孟玉楼是一位有钱的寡妇，比西门庆大三岁，颜值也不高，西门庆收编了孟玉楼之后，经济实力开始变得雄厚。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-652b7eddd65512d3f1049c1ebc9c1878_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"507\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-652b7eddd65512d3f1049c1ebc9c1878_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;507&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"507\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-652b7eddd65512d3f1049c1ebc9c1878_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-652b7eddd65512d3f1049c1ebc9c1878_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d4f04ee49b246c6e18151ee8fc6c6549_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"674\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d4f04ee49b246c6e18151ee8fc6c6549_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;674&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"674\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d4f04ee49b246c6e18151ee8fc6c6549_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d4f04ee49b246c6e18151ee8fc6c6549_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>第四颗龙珠就是<b>孙雪娥，</b>她原来是西门庆的丫鬟，被西门庆看上后做了妾，最后又跟仆人来旺私奔。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-0df6a45e216fd3b2cbc47c5acb19633d_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"533\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-0df6a45e216fd3b2cbc47c5acb19633d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;533&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"533\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-0df6a45e216fd3b2cbc47c5acb19633d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-0df6a45e216fd3b2cbc47c5acb19633d_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>而第五颗龙珠则是<b>潘金莲，</b>潘金莲大家就比较熟悉了，先嫁给了身高像郭敬明的武大郎，后来偶遇西门庆后被狂撩，于是就把武大给毒死，成功嫁给西门庆做了宠妾，成为他最重要的炮友。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6204452572e06efac638ab4f0293ae82_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"457\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6204452572e06efac638ab4f0293ae82_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;457&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"457\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6204452572e06efac638ab4f0293ae82_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6204452572e06efac638ab4f0293ae82_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>第六颗龙珠是<b>李瓶儿，</b>李瓶儿前夫花子虚是西门庆的好朋友，花子虚继承了太监叔叔的巨大遗产，而世界上最可怕的就是隔壁有老王。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b144705e89aeb3248181fdbba7b6b7b2_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"553\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b144705e89aeb3248181fdbba7b6b7b2_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;553&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"553\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b144705e89aeb3248181fdbba7b6b7b2_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b144705e89aeb3248181fdbba7b6b7b2_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>经过西门庆的一勾搭，顺利的把李瓶儿约进了优衣库试衣间，而花子虚又因为夜店逛太多，肾虚肾虚肾虚就死了，所以西门庆就顺利娶了李瓶儿，顺便继承了花子虚的<b>巨额财产</b>！</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2532c7d946bd8e87bee800f8d39ae63c_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"570\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2532c7d946bd8e87bee800f8d39ae63c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;570&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"570\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2532c7d946bd8e87bee800f8d39ae63c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2532c7d946bd8e87bee800f8d39ae63c_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>第七颗龙珠叫<b>庞春梅，</b>庞春梅原来就是吴月娘的丫鬟，后来被西门庆调拨给潘金莲使唤，成功的被西门庆收编为妾。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-74f9cd56026b9c9e96b42d02a6e42eb3_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"538\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-74f9cd56026b9c9e96b42d02a6e42eb3_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;538&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"538\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-74f9cd56026b9c9e96b42d02a6e42eb3_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-74f9cd56026b9c9e96b42d02a6e42eb3_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>你可能觉得西门庆好性福，其实这只是冰山一角，西门庆还和自己伙计的老婆王六儿，婢女宋惠莲、官太太林夫人，娱乐圈的李桂姐等等都有一腿，可以说是睡遍了半个县城，最后连<b>性别也不分了，</b>和自己的仆人、书童玩起了啪啪啪。 </p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-58cb4d6259bf832cc92634a11757aa4f_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"750\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-58cb4d6259bf832cc92634a11757aa4f_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;750&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"750\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-58cb4d6259bf832cc92634a11757aa4f_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-58cb4d6259bf832cc92634a11757aa4f_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>西门庆这么放纵身体扛不住，又从番僧那里得到了<b>神奇小药丸，</b>吃完之后完全控计不了计己，最后身体被掏空，精尽人亡，家道也从此开始衰落，而他的一帮妾们也开始了各自的生活。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-fafe58039213420709c9a50d21a286e2_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"487\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-fafe58039213420709c9a50d21a286e2_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;487&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"487\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-fafe58039213420709c9a50d21a286e2_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-fafe58039213420709c9a50d21a286e2_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>故事就是这么简单，然而兰陵笑笑生写了《金瓶梅》之后，历朝历代都把它定为一本禁书，但是越禁，在民间就越流行，而《金瓶梅》之所以那么火爆，很大程度是因为小说的内容<b>比较写实。</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-5057b43fe737ed2a7d2af52d7240ec2e_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"567\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-5057b43fe737ed2a7d2af52d7240ec2e_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;567&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"567\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-5057b43fe737ed2a7d2af52d7240ec2e_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-5057b43fe737ed2a7d2af52d7240ec2e_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>首先告诉了我们把妹的五字秘籍，<b>“潘、驴、邓、小、闲”，</b>像潘安一样帅气，驴一样有大行货，像邓通一样有钱，是个青春小鲜肉，最后还要有闲工夫陪伴，这样才能得到妹子的芳心，这在今天是不是依然也很适用呢？</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3fd98bb9dc6efe2266749daa224473d6_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"793\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3fd98bb9dc6efe2266749daa224473d6_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;793&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"793\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3fd98bb9dc6efe2266749daa224473d6_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3fd98bb9dc6efe2266749daa224473d6_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>其次揭露了西门庆发家致富的原因，首先是寻找到<b>强大政治依靠，</b>给东京<b>蔡太师</b>送礼并且认作干爹，获得了一个五品官阶的职务，成为了地方上有头有脸的人物。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-c90f136e6216f8752c1a8934d8a4b65b_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"387\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-c90f136e6216f8752c1a8934d8a4b65b_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;387&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"387\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-c90f136e6216f8752c1a8934d8a4b65b_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-c90f136e6216f8752c1a8934d8a4b65b_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>然后是靠傍富婆，强强联合，孟玉楼、李瓶儿虽然都是寡妇，但是架不住有钱呀，西门庆有了这些富婆的加盟，生意自然做的越来越大，这种<b>官商勾结，权钱交易</b>的手段，就是西门庆发家致富的原因。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-59777889f6ad91c35776c9e225d7554c_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"442\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-59777889f6ad91c35776c9e225d7554c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;442&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"442\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-59777889f6ad91c35776c9e225d7554c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-59777889f6ad91c35776c9e225d7554c_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>其次反映了人性的不同，例如西门庆在大老婆那里过夜，吴月娘就会劝诫丈夫要<b>好好做人，</b>而西门庆和潘金莲过夜，潘金莲就会要求买个架子床，买件貂，和今天小三要买LV包包是一样一样的。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-41d2f8e7d454c20e00dc058b1c3e0128_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"600\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-41d2f8e7d454c20e00dc058b1c3e0128_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;600&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"600\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-41d2f8e7d454c20e00dc058b1c3e0128_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-41d2f8e7d454c20e00dc058b1c3e0128_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>而在西门庆死后，吴月娘依然苦苦支撑家庭门面，李娇儿却立马卷钱回到了妓院，潘金莲和庞春梅则是为了找靠山，勾搭了<b>西门庆的女婿陈济敬，</b>这正是原配和小三之间的区别！ </p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f2ea90b12290bd96bfef7f250ac3b4ef_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"525\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f2ea90b12290bd96bfef7f250ac3b4ef_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;525&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"525\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f2ea90b12290bd96bfef7f250ac3b4ef_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f2ea90b12290bd96bfef7f250ac3b4ef_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>此外小说还直言不讳的告诉大家，<b>“钱能解决一切问题”！</b>即使干了很多坏事也无妨，西门庆就曾经嚣张的宣称：</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-98f007f14ae5ad2f1f781731d523609b_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"295\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-98f007f14ae5ad2f1f781731d523609b_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;295&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"295\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-98f007f14ae5ad2f1f781731d523609b_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-98f007f14ae5ad2f1f781731d523609b_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>这种金钱至上的观念，在今天的经济社会依然能引起<b>很大共鸣，</b>这也就是《金瓶梅》能火的原因！</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-35ec9d92e24ad592e42eb16ee183667c_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"503\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-35ec9d92e24ad592e42eb16ee183667c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;503&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"503\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-35ec9d92e24ad592e42eb16ee183667c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-35ec9d92e24ad592e42eb16ee183667c_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>虽然《金瓶梅》中最吸引大众眼球的，就是很多不可描述的黄段子，但是也有很多值得我们反思的故事，正如《金瓶梅》的序言里所说的，<b>一切还是在于读者本身。</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-5a7d3750f2919f58c553ef48ee6ce87e_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"174\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-5a7d3750f2919f58c553ef48ee6ce87e_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;             "content": "<p></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-95b40f69f57346f194482de97ef4699e_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"162\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-95b40f69f57346f194482de97ef4699e_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;162&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"162\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-95b40f69f57346f194482de97ef4699e_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-95b40f69f57346f194482de97ef4699e_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>一直以来，李白在教科书中的形象，总是狂傲潇洒、风流倜傥，绣口一吐就是半个盛唐！可以说李白在人们的心目中不仅是大唐诗人之光，更是中华文化的<b>王者荣耀！</b></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-33fb48d147eac175ef10b8f792e9384e_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-33fb48d147eac175ef10b8f792e9384e_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;640&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-33fb48d147eac175ef10b8f792e9384e_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-33fb48d147eac175ef10b8f792e9384e_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>在诗人论斤卖的大唐，李白为什么可以这么嚣张？侃爷这期就为大家，扒一扒李白的<b>诗仙成名之路。</b></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2789e762a47031a1e36469a65d8358e8_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"545\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2789e762a47031a1e36469a65d8358e8_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;545&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"545\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2789e762a47031a1e36469a65d8358e8_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2789e762a47031a1e36469a65d8358e8_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>公元742年，李白带着满腔意气来长安打拼。那年的大唐盛世繁华，那年的长安藏龙卧虎，竞争可以说是<b>十分激烈！</b></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c574d19bc9edbd4b24b0cb92c0e5fd5c_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c574d19bc9edbd4b24b0cb92c0e5fd5c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;640&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c574d19bc9edbd4b24b0cb92c0e5fd5c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c574d19bc9edbd4b24b0cb92c0e5fd5c_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>但李白自信他有<b>成名的资本。</b>首先他出身于一个富豪家庭，父亲李客是四川的大盐铁商，据历史学家郭沫若考证，长江沿岸三分之二的码头都是他们家的，可以说资产甩了杜甫几百条街！</p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6b36429596e8df24eb622452552b3685_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"567\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6b36429596e8df24eb622452552b3685_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;567&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"567\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6b36429596e8df24eb622452552b3685_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6b36429596e8df24eb622452552b3685_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>其次李白长着一张帅气的脸，他出生碎叶，相貌英俊，绝对的混血大帅哥。碎叶就是现在的<b>吉尔吉斯斯坦，</b>因此李白带有中东人的明显特征，感受一下差不多长这样——</p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-dd41e340c8a4d7e2ef38353533bde87f_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"540\" data-rawheight=\"766\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"540\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-dd41e340c8a4d7e2ef38353533bde87f_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;540&#39; height=&#39;766&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"540\" data-rawheight=\"766\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"540\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-dd41e340c8a4d7e2ef38353533bde87f_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-dd41e340c8a4d7e2ef38353533bde87f_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>当然，李白最引以为傲的还是——<b>才华！</b>李白五岁就开始学习儒家经典，后来又向赵蕤学道和纵横术，还得了一身的好剑法，绝对的文韬武略！</p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-eac2807a687c74384f651a806dc79cd8_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"900\" data-rawheight=\"86\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"900\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-eac2807a687c74384f651a806dc79cd8_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;900&#39; height=&#39;86&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"900\" data-rawheight=\"86\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"900\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-eac2807a687c74384f651a806dc79cd8_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-eac2807a687c74384f651a806dc79cd8_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2e331ee8c3c2c64a87be472f8f82012d_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"564\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2e331ee8c3c2c64a87be472f8f82012d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;564&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"564\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2e331ee8c3c2c64a87be472f8f82012d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2e331ee8c3c2c64a87be472f8f82012d_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>不过在唐代，商人的后代是<b>不能参加科举</b>的，所以李白就选择了另外一条路！</p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-746c20bd150c139d7af6b834d03c72f9_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"635\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-746c20bd150c139d7af6b834d03c72f9_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;635&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"635\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-746c20bd150c139d7af6b834d03c72f9_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-746c20bd150c139d7af6b834d03c72f9_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>当时的诗歌市场相当不错，大把权贵热衷于天使投资。宫廷正是这个市场<b>最高端的消费群体，</b>王维、张九龄、贺知章之类，哪个身后没有背景？不跟皇家发生点关系是很难出名的！</p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-70645ffaf7ba9e241e14eeaeb6e6897a_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-70645ffaf7ba9e241e14eeaeb6e6897a_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;640&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-70645ffaf7ba9e241e14eeaeb6e6897a_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-70645ffaf7ba9e241e14eeaeb6e6897a_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>那怎么跟宫廷发生关系呢？诗仙选择了——借位上势！看看李白的婚姻就知道了：李白的第一任妻子，是前宰相<b>许圉师的孙女，</b>第四任妻子是前宰相<b>宗楚客的孙女</b></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6606761d21c5e8ee84257d8b46d811fd_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"626\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6606761d21c5e8ee84257d8b46d811fd_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;626&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"626\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6606761d21c5e8ee84257d8b46d811fd_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6606761d21c5e8ee84257d8b46d811fd_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>凭借<b>老婆的人脉资源，</b>李白结识了很多达官贵人、贵妇名媛。比如宰相李林甫的女儿李朝空，从此进入唐朝上流社会</p><p>名气自然也就越来越大！</p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3b79a09053f2e3ac16c5f415d9205b85_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"526\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3b79a09053f2e3ac16c5f415d9205b85_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;526&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"526\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3b79a09053f2e3ac16c5f415d9205b85_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3b79a09053f2e3ac16c5f415d9205b85_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>其实李白的内心<b>最爱寡妇，</b>除了上面两段婚姻之外。李白和一位姓刘的寡妇同居了很久，后来他游历山东，又和一位寡妇开始了没羞没臊的生活，还生了一个小孩。</p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-620913c6debd607e8b4f3b9396f45c14_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"900\" data-rawheight=\"243\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"900\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-620913c6debd607e8b4f3b9396f45c14_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;900&#39; height=&#39;243&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"900\" data-rawheight=\"243\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"900\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-620913c6debd607e8b4f3b9396f45c14_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-620913c6debd607e8b4f3b9396f45c14_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>可是寡妇毕竟没有权势，要想成名还是得靠炒作。李白和很多美女闹过绯闻，比如说唐玄宗的妹妹玉真公主。通过绯闻女友的运作以及，好基友贺知章的倾情推荐。李白终于得到了唐玄宗的赏识，当了一个<b>翰林待诏，</b>主要负责给唐玄宗和杨贵妃写歌词。</p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-9090eb9808bed1ca127a632103e3254c_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"576\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-9090eb9808bed1ca127a632103e3254c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;576&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"576\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-9090eb9808bed1ca127a632103e3254c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-9090eb9808bed1ca127a632103e3254c_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>借裙带关系打入宫廷市场，只是成功的第一步，想要作品被广为传颂，关键还是在于能够直击每个人的心灵，所谓千穿万穿，马屁不穿，李白深深的明白这个道理，于是他<b>点赞狂魔</b>上身，开启了量产模式。</p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-e7d17d905752d621e7418949257c17ad_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"580\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-e7d17d905752d621e7418949257c17ad_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;580&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"580\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-e7d17d905752d621e7418949257c17ad_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-e7d17d905752d621e7418949257c17ad_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>当他出门旅游来到湖北<b>江山寺，</b>顺手就发朋友圈点赞，当地房价顿时暴涨。</p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-009f3e78bdf585bc63a8fe44686aae9e_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"900\" data-rawheight=\"71\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"900\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-009f3e78bdf585bc63a8fe44686aae9e_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;900&#39; height=&#39;71&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"900\" data-rawheight=\"71\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"900\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-009f3e78bdf585bc63a8fe44686aae9e_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-009f3e78bdf585bc63a8fe44686aae9e_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-8929ffabe0e992104fe9e691e09cde29_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"566\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-8929ffabe0e992104fe9e691e09cde29_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;566&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"566\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-8929ffabe0e992104fe9e691e09cde29_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-8929ffabe0e992104fe9e691e09cde29_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>当他来到酒店喝酒，不忘给美女老板吴姬点个赞，赞的如此清新脱俗，兰陵酒顿时价格暴增，直到现在依然是一个<b>知名品牌，</b>简直就是病毒式营销文案的典范。</p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a927d6828bca359c6cfd0f80b911a55d_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"900\" data-rawheight=\"152\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"900\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a927d6828bca359c6cfd0f80b911a55d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;900&#39; height=&#39;152&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"900\" data-rawheight=\"152\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"900\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a927d6828bca359c6cfd0f80b911a55d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a927d6828bca359c6cfd0f80b911a55d_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-701609aeb58b81670c08f7e011c3d57e_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"402\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-701609aeb58b81670c08f7e011c3d57e_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;402&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"402\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-701609aeb58b81670c08f7e011c3d57e_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-701609aeb58b81670c08f7e011c3d57e_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>当他结识文坛巨匠<b>孟浩然，</b>立马@孟浩然写诗夸赞。</p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-538504ddb6fb2f8e4169e6496cb008e1_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"900\" data-rawheight=\"78\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"900\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-538504ddb6fb2f8e4169e6496cb008e1_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;
